# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
Quantum Computation ^xGLUunUM

2018 - John Preskill: Noisy intermediate-scale quantum (NISQ) era.
Processors that contain about 50 to a few hundred of noisy qubits. ^jRmbtbnw

NISQ era ^jVoJeOHd

Variational Quantum Algorithms
- Variational Quantum Eigensolver (VQE)
- Quantum Approximate Optimization Algorithm (QAOA)
- Variational Quantum Machine Learning

Variational Algorithms are the most used in this era, but not the only ones.
Others:
- Quantum Annealing
- Gaussian boson sampling
- Analog quantum simulation
- Digital-analog quantum simulation
- ... ^I2oq8CDT

you assign control parameters to the qubits and logic gates, creating a variational algorithm ^791BbhWQ

Why NISQ devices? ^RUYtq08W

Consider the following circuit: ^NJb0rVkZ

If we apply 100 X-gates, the ideal result would be: ^kjViyyEw

When I have an odd number of gates X, I get the result -1 (|1⟩) and when it is even, I get 1 (|0⟩). ^rQGDFZtB

However, there are several types of errors.
- Coherent error: a control error that accumulates ^gVe4Zz51

- Bit-flip error ^559VH2yU

- Readout assignment error: reading error (ibm_washington: 7.6e-3) ^jVEFHsvB

The estimates of qubits for solving complex problems with quantum computing are: ^IUEvHsO8

quantum dynamics of a simples quantum magnet, 2D transverse field Ising model ^1aTSIuZt

analyze the activation energy of a catalyst for carbon fixation ^QH2NnzGV

factoring a large integer with Shor's algorithm ^hsCLxpTK

Quantum Machine Learning ^GRcJtuMZ

We can divide it in four groups. ^NEV1QEqd

data generating system ^PqcxUc7d

data processing system ^9SunkAKS

CC ^xLFPAonU

CQ ^nnFca2Ds

QC ^vb0z1WVa

QQ ^mleKj1ek

Focus: classical data processed in a quantum computer. ^IOsEX4MV

classical data in a classical computer ^d2cphcyH

quantum data in a classical computer ^rJiCHQcM

classical data in a quantum computer ^xD55HGwA

quantum data in a quantum computer ^ZWAhKwXW

não é trivial pois dados quânticos, em geral, tem uma quantidade muito grande de informação e em alguns casos nem é possível. ^bDGkOpxI

training data ^LVndniiQ

model ^3Kw75tZS

cost function ^Wqjt7vwm

update ^zxA6M6Zw

compute gradients ^3081WU6b

We change the classical model for a variational circuit. ^YICRpD5f

Steps for training:
1. Encode classical data into a quantum state
    - Basis encoding
    - Amplitude encoding
    - Angle encoding

2. Apply a parameterized model
    - It's an ongoing study. 
    - It's possible to make a classic optimization, you won't find a global minimum, but might find a minimum.

3. Measure the qubits to get the labels ^YNWKAJtF

Quantum Machine Learning Zoo ^E7zLrP6J

It's possible to use a variational algorithm to develop a hyperplane separator, as in an SVM. ^cgJ3dIjC

the encoding process plays the role of the Feature Map ^Ovr5NzhD

some way to adjust the hyperplane ^Vo2GCuoq

Just like in SVM, we can rewrite this problem as a dual, so that the whole problem is to calculate the kernel.
It's possible to implement the Quantum Kernel Estimator in a quantum computer.
The main ideia is to find a feature map that is more efficient than classics feature maps. ^LzH9lNOh

Non-linearity in a quantum model ^6WQuaTxI

The measurement introduces non-linearity. ^CXdE3OiX

Another model to include non-linearity. ^GOm0CoZA

Quantum Neural Network ^VQEKeWSe

The introduction of multiple qubits may improve its performance as more hidden layers improve the classification task of an artificial neural network. ^pPduWBo6

It's possible to use only one qubit, since it is continuous, dividing its space into regions. ^K3gwl7q6

Universality of a quantum model ^IBDdEgPD

A neural network can describe any function, and you can describe it as a Fourier Series. You can also describe any function as a quantum circuit. ^U3UwLQFy

CNN Quantum Filter ^nudfdwKk

Generators for GAN ^TiuS3Rn5

Replace the data Generator for a quantum algorithm. ^C3fjeo08
